Source Code

These source-code files were transcribed from scans made from Don Eyles's personal copy of Luminary 069. They were scanned at archive.org's Boston facility, and the scanning was sponsored by Onno Hommes. The code was transcribed from these scans by a team of volunteers who are referenced in the program comments. Comments from the original source code are prefixed with a single '#' symbol, whereas comments added later are prefixed by "##" or "###". In some cases, where similar code blocks exist in previously-transcribed AGC programs (primarily Luminary 99, from Apollo 11) those code blocks were used as a starting point and then corrected to agree with the Luminary 69 scans. The full scans are available at the Virtual AGC project's collection at archive.org, while more-convenient reduced-size (but reduced-quality) images are available at the main Virtual AGC website. Report any errors noted by creating an issue report at the Virtual AGC project's GitHub repository. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 069 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-011
	19:02 NOV. 25,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

017473,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.
017474,000003:                                                                                                  ## Filename:    PINBALL_GAME__BUTTONS_AND_LIGHTS.agc
017475,000004:                                                                                                  ## Purpose:     The main source file for Luminary revision 069.
017476,000005:                                                                                                  ##              It is part of the source code for the original release
017477,000006:                                                                                                  ##              of the flight software for the Lunar Module's (LM) Apollo
017478,000007:                                                                                                  ##              Guidance Computer (AGC) for Apollo 10. The actual flown
017479,000008:                                                                                                  ##              version was Luminary 69 revision 2, which included a
017480,000009:                                                                                                  ##              newer lunar gravity model and only affected module 2.
017481,000010:                                                                                                  ##              This file is intended to be a faithful transcription, except
017482,000011:                                                                                                  ##              that the code format has been changed to conform to the
017483,000012:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the
017484,000013:                                                                                                  ##              original YUL assembler.
017485,000014:                                                                                                  ## Reference:   pp. 403-484
017486,000015:                                                                                                  ## Assembler:   yaYUL

017500,000029:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
017501,000030:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 4      DATE - 27 APRIL 1967      ASSEMBLY - PINDANCE REV 18
017502,000031:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY - FILENE
017503,000032:                                                                                                  #  LOG SECTION - PINBALL GAME  BUTTONS AND LIGHTS
017504,000033: 
017505,000034:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
017506,000035: 
017507,000036:                                                                                                  #     THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM PROGRAM OPERATES UNDER EXECUTIVE
017508,000037:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL AND PROCESSES INFORMATION EXCHANGED BETWEEN THE AGC AND THE
017509,000038:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER OPERATOR.  THE INPUTS TO THE PROGRAM ARE FROM THE KEYBOARD,
017510,000039:                                                                                                  #  FROM INTERNAL PROGRAMS, AND FROM THE UPLINK.
017511,000040:                                                                                                  #     THE LANGUAGE OF COMMUNICATION WITH THE PROGRAM IS A PAIR OF WORDS
017512,000041:                                                                                                  #  KNOWN AS VERB AND NOUN.  EACH OF THESE IS REPRESENTED BY A 2 CHARACTER
017513,000042:                                                                                                  #  DECIMAL NUMBER.  THE VERB CODE INDICATES WHAT ACTION IS TO BE TAKEN, THE
017514,000043:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE INDICATES TO WHAT THIS ACTION IS APPLIED.  NOUNS USUALLY
017515,000044:                                                                                                  #  REFER TO A GROUP OF ERASABLE REGISTERS.
017516,000045: 
017517,000046:                                                                                                  #  VERBS ARE GROUPED INTO DISPLAYS, LOADS, MONITORS (DISPLAYS THAT ARE
017518,000047:                                                                                                  #  UPDATED ONCE PER SECOND), SPECIAL FUNCTIONS, AND EXTENDED VERBS(THESE
017519,000048:                                                                                                  #  ARE OUTSIDE OF THE DOMAIN OF PINBALL AND CAN BE FOUND UNDER LOG SECTION
017520,000049:                                                                                                  #  :EXTENDED VERBS:).
017521,000050:                                                                                                  #  A LIST OF VERBS AND NOUNS IS GIVEN IN LOG SECTION :ASSEMBLY AND 
017522,000051:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION INFORMATION:.
017523,000052:

Ramón Alonso, one of the original AGC developers, provides a little more insight: Apparently, nobody had yet arrived at any kind of software requirements for the AGC's user interface when the desire arose within the Instrumentation Laboratory to set up a demo guidance-computer unit with which to impress visitors to the lab. Of course, this demo would have to do something, if it was going to be at all impressive, and to do something it would need some software. In short order, some of the coders threw together a demo program, inventing and using the verb/noun user-interface concept (in the whimsical fashion seen in much of this code), but without any idea that the verb/noun concept would somehow survive into the flight software. As time passed, and more and more people became familiar with the demo, nobody got around to inventing an improvement for the user interface, so the coders simply built it into the flight software without any specific requirements to do so.

However, that does not mean that the verb/noun interface was universally beloved. Ramón says that many objections were received from naysayers, such as "it's not scientific", "it's not dignified", or even "astronauts won't understand it". Even though the coders of the demo hadn't seriously intended the verb/noun interface to be used in any permanent way, it became a kind of devilish game to counter these objections with (perhaps) sophistic arguments as to why the interface was really a good one. In the end, the coders won. I don't know whether they were elated or dismayed by this victory.

The astronauts, of course, could understand the interface, but they did not like it. Most of them really wanted an interface much more like that they had used in aircraft: i.e., lots of dials and switches. Dave Scott is the the only astronaut I'm aware of who had kind words for it (or for the AGC in general), though we are told that Jim McDivitt wasn't necessary completely hostile to it.

—Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017558,000087: 
017559,000088:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCES-
017560,000089: 
017561,000090:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD:
017562,000091:                                                                                                  #     EACH DEPRESSION OF A KEYBOARD BUTTON ACTIVATES INTERRUPT KEYRUPT1
017563,000092:                                                                                                  #  AND PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO CHANNEL 15.  KEYRUPT1 PLACES THE KEY
017564,000093:                                                                                                  #  CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY
017565,000094:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (AT :CHARIN:), AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017566,000095: 
017567,000096:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK:
017568,000097:                                                                                                  #     EACH WORD RECEIVED BY THE UPLINK ACTIVATES INTERRUPT UPRUPT WHICH
017569,000098:                                                                                                  #  PLACES THE 5 BIT KEY CODE INTO MPAC, ENTERS AN EXECUTIVE REQUEST FOR THE
017570,000099:                                                                                                  #  KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM (AT:CHARIN:) AND EXECUTES A RESUME.
017571,000100: 
017572,000101:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS:
017573,000102:                                                                                                  #     INTERNAL PROGRAMS CALL PINBALL AT :NVSUB: WITH THE DESIRED VERB/NOUN
017574,000103:                                                                                                  #  CODE IN A (LOW 7 BITS FOR NOUN, NEXT 7 BITS FOR VERB).  DETAILS
017575,000104:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBED ON REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE
017576,000105:                                                                                                  #  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017577,000106: 
017578,000107:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
017579,000108:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY EXTERNAL ACTION, THERE ARE FOUR EXITS:
017580,000109:                                                                                                  #           1) ALL BUT (2), (3), AND (4) EXIT DIRECTLY TO ENDOFJOB.
017581,000110:                                                                                                  #           2) EXTENDED VERBS GO TO THE EXTENDED VERB FAN AS PART OF THE

Page 404 

017583,000112:                                                                                                  #              PINBALL EXECUTIVE JOB WITH PRIORITY 30000.  IT IS THE 
017584,000113:                                                                                                  #              RESPONSIBILITY OF THE EXTENDED VERB CALLED TO EVENTUALLY
017585,000114:                                                                                                  #              CHANGE PRIORITY (IF NECESSARY) AND DO AN ENDOFJOB.
017586,000115:                                                                                                  #              ALSO PINBALL IS A NOVAC JOB. EBANK SET FOR COMMON.
017587,000116:                                                                                                  #           3) VERB 37. CHANGE OF PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) CALLS :V37: IN THE
017588,000117:                                                                                                  #              SERVICE ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO
017589,000118:                                                                                                  #              30000.  THE NEW PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IS LEFT IN A.
017590,000119:                                                                                                  #           4) KEY RELEASE BUTTON CALLS :PINBRNCH: IN THE DISPLAY INTERFACE
017591,000120:                                                                                                  #              ROUTINES AS PART OF THE PINBALL EXEC JOB WITH PRIO 30000 IF 
017592,000121:                                                                                                  #              THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IS OFF AND :CADRSTOR: IS NOT +0.
017593,000122: 
017594,000123:                                                                                                  #     IF PINBALL WAS CALLED BY INTERNAL PROGRAMS, EXIT FROM PINBALL IS BACK
017595,000124:                                                                                                  #  TO CALLING ROUTINE.  DETAILS DESCRIBED IN REMARKS CARDS JUST BEFORE
017596,000125:                                                                                                  #  :NVSUB: AND :NVSBWAIT: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBERS).
017597,000126: 
017598,000127: 
017599,000128:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
017600,000129: 
017601,000130:                                                                                                  #  EXTERNAL INITIATION:
017602,000131:                                                                                                  #     IF SOME IMPROPER SEQUENCE OF KEY CODES IS DETECTED, THE OPERATOR
017603,000132:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT IS TURNED ON AND EXIT IS TO :ENDOFJOB:.
017604,000133: 
017605,000134:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAM INITIATION:
017606,000135:                                                                                                  #     IF AN ILLEGAL V/N COMBINATION IS ATTEMPTED, AN ABORT IS CAUSED
017607,000136:                                                                                                  #  (WITH OCTAL 01501).
017608,000137:                                                                                                  #     IF A SECOND ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL, AN ABORT IS
017609,000138:                                                                                                  #  CAUSED (WITH OCTAL 01206). THERE ARE TWO WAYS TO GO TO SLEEP IN PINBALL:
017610,000139:                                                                                                  #           1) ENDIDLE OR DATAWAIT.
017611,000140:                                                                                                  #           2) NVSBWAIT, PRENVBSY, OR NVSUBUSY.
017612,000141: 
017613,000142:                                                                                                  #  CONDITIONS LEADING TO THE ABOVE ARE DESCRIBED IN FORTHCOMING MIT/IL
017614,000143:                                                                                                  #  E-REPORT DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017615,000144: 
017616,000145: 
017617,000146:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT-
017618,000147: 
017619,000148:                                                                                                  #     INFORMATION TO BE SENT TO THE DISPLAY PANEL IS LEFT IN THE :DSPTAB:
017620,000149:                                                                                                  #  BUFFERS REGISTERS (UNDER EXEC CONTROL).  :DSPOUT: (A PART OF T4RUPT)
017621,000150:                                                                                                  #  HANDLES THE PLACING OF THE :DSPTAB: INFORMATION INTO OUTPUT CHANNEL 10
017622,000151:                                                                                                  #  IN INTERRUPT.
017623,000152: 
017624,000153: 
017625,000154:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION-
017626,000155: 
017627,000156:                                                                                                  #     FRESH START AND RESTART INITIALIZE THE NECESSARY E REGISTERS FOR
017628,000157:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IN :STARTSUB:.   REGISTERS ARE:  DSPTAB BUFFER, CADRSTOR,
017629,000158:                                                                                                  #  REQRET, CLPASS, DSPLOCK, MONSAVE, MONSAVE1, VERBREG, NOUNREG, DSPLIST,
017630,000159:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT, NOUT.
017631,000160: 
017632,000161:                                                                                                  #  A COMPLETE LIST OF ALL THE ERASABLES (BOTH RESERVED AND TEMPORARIES) FOR

Page 405 

017634,000163:                                                                                                  #  PINBALL IS GIVEN BELOW.
017635,000164: 
017636,000165: 
017637,000166:                                                                                                  #  THE FOLLOWING ARE OF GENERAL INTEREST-
017638,000167: 
017639,000168:                                                                                                  #     REMARKS CARDS PRECEDE THE REFERENCED SYMBOL DEFINITION.  SEE SYMBOL
017640,000169:                                                                                                  #  TABLE TO FIND APPROPRIATE PAGE NUMBERS.
017641,000170: 
017642,000171:                                                                                                  #     NVSUB   CALLING POINT FOR INTERNAL USE OF PINBALL.
017643,000172:                                                                                                  #               OF RELATED INTEREST   NVSBWAIT
017644,000173:                                                                                                  #                                     NVSUBUSY
017645,000174:                                                                                                  #                                     PRENVBSY
017646,000175: 
017647,000176:                                                                                                  #     ENDIDLE   ROUTINE FOR INTERNAL PROGRAMS WISHING TO GO TO SLEEP WHILE
017648,000177:                                                                                                  #               AWAITING OPERATORS RESPONSE.
017649,000178: 
017650,000179:                                                                                                  #     DSPMM   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY DISPLAY A DECIMAL
017651,000180:                                                                                                  #             PROGRAM CODE (MAJOR MODE) IN THE PROGRAM (MAJOR MODE) LIGHTS.
017652,000181:                                                                                                  #             (DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY DIRECTLY BUT ENTERS EXEC REQUEST
017653,000182:                                                                                                  #             FOR DSPMMJB WITH PRIO 30000 AND RETURNS TO CALLER.)
017654,000183: 
017655,000184:                                                                                                  #     BLANKSUB   ROUTINE BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY BLANK ANY
017656,000185:                                                                                                  #                COMBINATION OF THE DISPLAY REGISTERS R1, R2, R3.
017657,000186: 
017658,000187:                                                                                                  #     JAMTERM   ROUTINES BY WHICH AN INTERNAL PROGRAM MAY PERFORM THE
017659,000188:                                                                                                  #     JAMPROC   TERMINATE (V 34) OR PROCEED (V 33) FUNCTION.
017660,000189: 
017661,000190:                                                                                                  #     MONITOR   VERBS FOR PERIODIC ( 1 PER SEC) DISPLAY.
017662,000191: 
017663,000192:                                                                                                  #     PLEASE PERFORM, PLEASE MARK SITUATIONS
017664,000193:                                                                                                  #                  REMARKS DESCRIBING HOW AN INTERNAL ROUTINE SHOULD HANDLE
017665,000194:                                                                                                  #                  THESE SITUATIONS CAN BE FOUND JUST BEFORE :NVSUB: (SEE
017666,000195:                                                                                                  #                  SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017667,000196: 
017668,000197:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLE FORMAT IS DESCRIBED ON A PAGE OF REMARKS CARDS JUST
017669,000198:                                                                                                  #     BEFORE :DSPABC: (SEE SYMBOL TABLE FOR PAGE NUMBER).
017670,000199: 
017671,000200:                                                                                                  #     THE NOUN TABLES THEMSELVES ARE FOUND IN LOG SECTION :PINBALL NOUN
017672,000201:                                                                                                  #     TABLES:.
017673,000202: 
017674,000203: 
017675,000204:                                                                                                  #  FOR FURTHER DETAILS ABOUT OPERATION OF THE KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM
017676,000205:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM, SEE THE MISSION PLAN AND/OR MIT/IL E-2129
017677,000206:                                                                                                  #  DESCRIBING KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY OPERATION FOR 278.
017678,000207:

The document described above, "Keyboard and Display Program Operation" by Alan I. Green and Robert J. Filene is available online at the Virtual AGC website. —Ron Burkey, 07/2009

017700,000229:                                                                                                  #  RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION
017701,000230: 
017702,000231:                                                                                                  #  DSPCOUNT ERASE                  DISPLAY POSITION INDICATOR
017703,000232:                                                                                                  #  DECBRNCH ERASE                  +DEC, - DEC, OCT INDICATOR
017704,000233:                                                                                                  #  VERBREG  ERASE                  VERB CODE
017705,000234:                                                                                                  #  NOUNREG  ERASE                  NOUN CODE
017706,000235:                                                                                                  #  XREG     ERASE                  R1 INPUT BUFFER
017707,000236:                                                                                                  #  YREG     ERASE                  R2 INPUT BUFFER
017708,000237:                                                                                                  #  ZREG     ERASE                  R3 INPUT BUFFER
017709,000238:                                                                                                  #  XREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF XREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017710,000239:                                                                                                  #  YREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF YREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017711,000240:                                                                                                  #  HITEMOUT =      YREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017712,000241:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = LOTEMOUT-1.
017713,000242:                                                                                                  #  ZREGLP   ERASE                  LO PART OF ZREG (FOR DEC CONV ONLY)
017714,000243:                                                                                                  #  LOTEMOUT =      ZREGLP          TEMP FOR DISPLAY OF HRS, MIN, SEC
017715,000244:                                                                                                  #                                           MUST = HITEMOUT+1.
017716,000245:                                                                                                  #  MODREG   ERASE                  MODE CODE
017717,000246:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK  ERASE                  KEYBOARD/SUBROUTINE CALL INTERLOCK
017718,000247:                                                                                                  #  REQRET   ERASE                  RETURN REGISTER FOR LOAD
017719,000248:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT ERASE                  STATUS INDICATOR FOR LOADTST
017720,000249:                                                                                                  #  CLPASS   ERASE                  PASS INDICATOR CLEAR
017721,000250:                                                                                                  #  NOUT     ERASE                  ACTIVITY COUNTER FOR DSPTAB
017722,000251:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR ERASE                  MACHINE CADR FOR NOUN
017723,000252:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE  ERASE                  N/V CODE FOR MONITOR. (= MONSAVE1-1)
017724,000253:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 ERASE                  NOUNCADR FOR MONITOR (MATBS) =MONSAVE+1
017725,000254:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE2 ERASE                  NVMONOPT OPTIONS
017726,000255:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB   ERASE          +13D    0-10,DISPLAY PANEL BUFFER.11-13,C RELAYS
017727,000256:                                                                                                  #  CADRSTOR ERASE                  ENDIDLE STORAGE
017728,000257:                                                                                                  #  NVQTEM   ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING ADDRESS
017729,000258:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVBNKTEM-1
017730,000259:                                                                                                  #  NVBNKTEM ERASE                  NVSUB STORAGE FOR CALLING BANK
017731,000260:                                                                                                  #                                  MUST = NVQTEM+1
017732,000261:                                                                                                  #  VERBSAVE ERASE                  NEEDED FOR RECYCLE
017733,000262:                                                                                                  #  DSPLIST  ERASE                  WAITING REG FOR DSP SYST INTERNAL USE
017734,000263:                                                                                                  #  EXTVBACT REASE                  EXTENDED VERB ACTIVITY INTERLOCK
017735,000264:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM1  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 1 (MOSTLY FOR TIME)
017736,000265:                                                                                                  #  DSPTEM2  ERASE          +2      BUFFER STORAGE AREA 2 (MOSTLY FOR DEG)
017737,000266:                                                                                                  #  END OF ERASABLES RESERVED FOR PINBALL EXECUTIVE ACTION

017844,000373:                                                                                                  #  THE INPUT CODES ASSUMED FOR THE KEYBOARD ARE,
017845,000374:                                                                                                  #  0        10000
017846,000375:                                                                                                  #  1        00001
017847,000376:                                                                                                  #  9        01001
017848,000377:                                                                                                  #  VERB     10001
017849,000378:                                                                                                  #  ERROR RES10010
017850,000379:                                                                                                  #  KEY RLSE 11001
017851,000380:                                                                                                  #  +        11010
017852,000381:                                                                                                  #  -        11011
017853,000382:                                                                                                  #  ENTER    11100
017854,000383:                                                                                                  #  CLEAR    11110
017855,000384:                                                                                                  #  NOUN     11111

2003 RSB — The PROCEED key has no keycode; it is read by an alternate mechanism. 

017857,000386: 
017858,000387: 
017859,000388:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT FORMAT FOR DISPLAY PANEL. SET OUT0 TO  AAAABCCCCCDDDDD.
017860,000389:                                                                                                  #  A-S SELECT A RELAYWORD. THIS DETERMINES WHICH PAIR OF CHARACTERS ARE
017861,000390:                                                                                                  #  ENERGIZED.
017862,000391:                                                                                                  #  B FOR SPECIAL RELAYS SUCH AS SIGNS ETC.
017863,000392:                                                                                                  #  C-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR LEFT CHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD
017864,000393:                                                                                                  #  D-S  5 BIT RELAY CODE FOR RIGHTCHAR OF PAIR SELECTED BY RELAYWORD.
017865,000394: 
017866,000395:                                                                                                  #  THE PANEL APPEARS AS FOLLOWS,
017867,000396:                                                                                                  #  MD1    MD2                         (MAJOR MODE)
017868,000397:                                                                                                  #  VD1    VD2 (VERB)    ND1    ND2    (NOUN)
017869,000398:                                                                                                  #  R1D1   R1D2   R1D3   R1D4   R1D5   (R1)
017870,000399:                                                                                                  #  R2D1   R2D2   R2D3   R2D4   R2D5   (R2)
017871,000400:                                                                                                  #  R3D1   R3D2   R3D3   R3D4   R3D5   (R3)
017872,000401: 
017873,000402:                                                                                                  #  EACH OF THESE IS GIVEN A DSPCOUNT NUMBER FOR USE WITHIN COMPUTATION ONLY
017874,000403:                                                                                                  #  MD1   25     R2D1  11         ALL ARE OCTAL
017875,000404:                                                                                                  #  MD2   24     R2D2  10
017876,000405:                                                                                                  #  VD1   23     R2D3   7
017877,000406:                                                                                                  #  VD2   22     R2D4   6
017878,000407:                                                                                                  #  ND1   21     R2D5   5
017879,000408:                                                                                                  #  ND2   20     R3D1   4
017880,000409:                                                                                                  #  R1D1  16     R3D2   3
017881,000410:                                                                                                  #  R1D2  15     R3D3   2
017882,000411:                                                                                                  #  R1D3  14     R3D4   1
017883,000412:                                                                                                  #  R1D4  13     R3D5   0
017884,000413:                                                                                                  #  R1D5  12
017885,000414: 
017886,000415: 
017887,000416:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS AN 11 REGISTER TABLE (DSPTAB) FOR THE DISPLAY PANEL.
017888,000417: 
017889,000418:                                                                                                  #  DSPTAB RELAYWD       BIT11     BITS 10-6     BITS 5-1
017890,000419:                                                                                                  #  RELADD
017891,000420:                                                                                                  #  10     1011                    MD1  (25)     MD2  (24)
017892,000421:                                                                                                  #  9      1010                    VD1  (23)     VD2  (22)
017893,000422:                                                                                                  #  8      1001                    ND1  (21)     ND2  (20)
017894,000423:                                                                                                  #  7      1000                                  R1D1 (16)

Page 410 

017896,000425:                                                                                                  #  6      0111          +R1       R1D2 (15)     R1D3 (14)
017897,000426:                                                                                                  #  5      0110          -R1       R1D4 (13)     R1D5 (12)
017898,000427:                                                                                                  #  4      0101          +R2       R2D1 (11)     R2D2 (10)
017899,000428:                                                                                                  #  3      0100          -R2       R2D3 (7)      R2D4 (6)
017900,000429:                                                                                                  #  2      0011                    R2D5 (5)      R3D1 (4)
017901,000430:                                                                                                  #  1      0010          +R3       R3D2 (3)      R3D3 (2)
017902,000431:                                                                                                  #  0      0001          -R3       R3D4 (1)      R3D5 (0)
017903,000432:                                                                                                  #         0000   NO RELAYWORD
017904,000433: 
017905,000434: 
017906,000435:                                                                                                  #  THE 5 BIT OUTPUT RELAY CODES ARE:
017907,000436:                                                                                                  #  BLANK      00000
017908,000437:                                                                                                  #  0          10101
017909,000438:                                                                                                  #  1          00011
017910,000439:                                                                                                  #  2          11001
017911,000440:                                                                                                  #  3          11011
017912,000441:                                                                                                  #  4          01111
017913,000442:                                                                                                  #  5          11110
017914,000443:                                                                                                  #  6          11100
017915,000444:                                                                                                  #  7          10011
017916,000445:                                                                                                  #  8          11101
017917,000446:                                                                                                  #  9          11111
017918,000447: 
017919,000448: 
017920,000449:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT BITS USED BY PINBALL:
017921,000450: 
017922,000451:                                                                                                  #             KEY RELEASE LIGHT    - BIT 5 OF CHANNEL 11
017923,000452:                                                                                                  #             VERB/NOUN FLASH      - BIT 6 OF CHANNEL 11
017924,000453:                                                                                                  #             OPERATOR ERROR LIGHT - BIT 7 OF CHANNEL 11
017925,000454:

018633,001162:

Page 426 

018635,001164:                                                                                                  #           NOUN   TABLES
018636,001165:                                                                                                  #  NOUN CODE L/40, NORMAL NOUN CASE.  NOUN CODE G/E 40, MIXED NOUN CASE.
018637,001166:                                                                                                  #  FOR NORMAL CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE       ECADR     FOR EACH NOUN.
018638,001167:                                                                                                  #  +0 INDICATES NOUN NOT USED.   - ENTRY INDICATES MACHINE CADR(E OR F) TO
018639,001168:                                                                                                  #  BE SPECIFIED. -1 INDICATES CHANNEL TO BE SPECIFIED. -0 INDICATES AUGMENT
018640,001169:                                                                                                  #  OF LAST MACHINE CADR SUPPLIED.
018641,001170: 
018642,001171:                                                                                                  #  FOR MIXED CASE, NNADTAB CONTAINS ONE INDIRECT ADDRESS(IDADDREL) IN LOW
018643,001172:                                                                                                  #  10 BITS, AND THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER IN THE HIGH 5 BITS.
018644,001173: 
018645,001174:                                                                                                  #  NNTYPTAB IS A PACKED TABLE OF THE FORM MMMMMNNNNNPPPPP.
018646,001175: 
018647,001176:                                                                                                  #  FOR THE NORMAL CASE, M-S ARE THE COMPONENT CODE NUMBER.
018648,001177:                                                                                                  #                       N-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE CODE NUMBER.
018649,001178:                                                                                                  #                       P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT CODE NUMBER.
018650,001179: 
018651,001180:                                                                                                  #  MIXED CASE,M-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018652,001181:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER
018653,001182:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018654,001183:                                                                                                  #             N-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018655,001184:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER
018656,001185:                                                                                                  #             P-S ARE THE SF CONSTANT1 CODE NUMBER      1 COMPONENT CASE
018657,001186: 
018658,001187:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO AN INDIRECT ADDRESS TABLE(IDADDTAB) FOR MIXED CASE ONLY.
018659,001188:                                                                                                  #  EACH ENTRY CONTAINS ONE ECADR.    IDADDREL IS THE RELATIVE ADDRESS OF
018660,001189:                                                                                                  #  THE FIRST OF THESE ENTRIES.
018661,001190:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ONE ENTRY IN THIS TABLE FOR EACH COMPONENT OF A MIXED NOUN
018662,001191:                                                                                                  #  THEY ARE LISTED IN ORDER OF ASCENDING K.
018663,001192: 
018664,001193:                                                                                                  #  THERE IS ALSO A SCALE FACTOR ROUTINE NUMBER TABLE( RUTMXTAB ) FOR MIXED
018665,001194:                                                                                                  #  CASE ONLY. THERE IS ONE ENTRY PER MIXED NOUN. THE FORM IS,
018666,001195:                                                                                                  #        QQQQQRRRRRSSSSS
018667,001196:                                                                                                  #  Q-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 3 CODE NUMBER     3 COMPONENT CASE
018668,001197:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER
018669,001198:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018670,001199:                                                                                                  #  R-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 2 CODE NUMBER     2 COMPONENT CASE
018671,001200:                                                                                                  #  S-S ARE THE SF ROUTINE 1 CODE NUMBER
018672,001201: 
018673,001202: 
018674,001203:                                                                                                  #  IN OCTAL DISPLAY AND LOAD (OCT OR DEC) VERBS, EXCLUDE USE OF VERBS WHOSE
018675,001204:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT NUMBER IS GREATER THAN THE NUMBER OF COMPONENTS IN NOUN.
018676,001205:                                                                                                  #  (ALL MACHINE ADDRESS TO BE SPECIFIED NOUNS ARE 3 COMPONENT.)
018677,001206: 
018678,001207: 
018679,001208:                                                                                                  #  IN MULTI-COMPONENT LOAD VERBS, NO MIXING OF OCTAL AND DECIMAL DATA
018680,001209:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT WORDS IS ALLOWED. ALARM IF VIOLATION.
018681,001210: 
018682,001211:                                                                                                  #  IN DECIMAL LOADS OF DATA, 5 NUMERICAL CHARACTERS MUST BE KEYED IN
018683,001212:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE EACH ENTER. IF NOT, ALARM.
018684,001213:

Page 427 

018686,001215:                                                                                                  #           DISPLAY  VERBS
018687,001216: 41,2353           44752        DSPABC             CS       TWO                                   
018688,001217: 41,2354           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
018689,001218: 41,2355           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD                               
018690,001219: 41,2356           40002                           CS       2                                     
018691,001220: 41,2357           56132                           XCH      BUF        +2                         
018692,001221: 41,2360           44753        DSPAB              CS       ONE                                   
018693,001222: 41,2361           02424                           TC       COMPTEST                              
018694,001223: 41,2362           50145                           INDEX    NOUNADD

019831,002360:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ALLOWS OTHER KEYBOARD ACTIVITY. IT IS ENDED BY VERB TERMINATE,
019832,002361:                                                                                                  #  VERB PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, VERB RESEQUENCE,
019833,002362:                                                                                                  #  ANOTHER MONITOR, OR ANY NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES THE DSPLOCK (PROVIDED
019834,002363:                                                                                                  #  THAT THE OPERATOR HAS SOMEHOW ALLOWED THE ENDING OF A MONITOR WHICH
019835,002364:                                                                                                  #  HE HAS INITIATED THROUGH THE KEYBOARD).
019836,002365: 
019837,002366:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR ACTION IS SUSPENDED, BUT NOT ENDED, BY ANY KEYBOARD ACTION,
019838,002367:                                                                                                  #  EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET. IT BEGINS AGAIN WHEN KEY RELEASE IS PERFORMED.
019839,002368:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SAVES THE NOUN AND APPROPRIATE DISPLAY VERB IN MONSAVE. IT SAVES
019840,002369:                                                                                                  #  NOUNCADR IN MONSAVE1, IF NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. BIT 15 OF
019841,002370:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE1 IS THE KILL MONITOR SIGNAL (KILLER BIT). BIT 14 OF MONSAVE1
019842,002371:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES THE CURRENT MONITOR WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED (EXTERNAL
019843,002372:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR BIT). IT IS TURNED OFF BY RELDSP AND KILMONON.
019844,002373: 
019845,002374:                                                                                                  #  MONSAVE INDICATES IF MONITOR IS ON(+=ON, +0=OFF)
019846,002375:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +, MONITOR ENTERS NO REQUEST, BUT TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019847,002376:                                                                                                  #  IF MONSAVE IS +0, MONITOR ENTERS REQUEST AND TURNS KILLER BIT OFF.
019848,002377: 
019849,002378:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB (IF EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT IS OFF), VB=PROCEED WITHOUT DATA,
019850,002379:                                                                                                  #  VB=RESEQUENCE, AND VB=TERMINATE TURN KILL MONITOR BIT ON.
019851,002380: 
019852,002381:                                                                                                  #  IF KILLER BIT IS ON, MONREQ ENTERS NO FURTHER REQUESTS, ZEROS MONSAVE
019853,002382:                                                                                                  #  AND MONSAVE1 (TURNING OFF KILLER BIT AND EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT).
019854,002383: 
019855,002384:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR DOSENT TEST FOR MATBS SINCE NVSUB CAN HANDLE INTERNAL MATBS NOW

019982,002511:                                                                                                  #  DSPFMEM IS USED TO DISPLAY (IN OCTAL) ANY FIXED REGISTER.
019983,002512:                                                                                                  #  IT IS USED WITH NOUN = MACHINE CADR TO BE SPECIFIED. THE FCADR OF THE 
019984,002513:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED LOCATION IS THEN PUNCHED IN. IT HANDLES F/F (FCADR 4000-7777)
019985,002514: 
019986,002515:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27, THIS IS ENOUGH.
019987,002516: 
019988,002517:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30, THE THIRD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26 (PRIO, ADRES, BBCON)
019989,002518:                                                                                                  #  MUST BE PRELOADED WITH THE DESIRED SUPERBANK BITS (BITS 5,6,7).
019990,002519:                                                                                                  #           V23N26 SHOULD BE USED.
019991,002520: 
019992,002521:                                                                                                  #  SUMMARY
019993,002522:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS L/E 27,                          V27N01E(FCADR)E
019994,002523:                                                                                                  #  FOR BANKS G/E 30,    V23N26E(SUPERBITS)E   V27N01E(FCADR)E
019995,002524: 
019996,002525: 41,3353           34317        DSPFMEM            CAF      R1D1                                  #  IF F/F, DATACALL USES BANK 02 OR 03.
019997,002526: 41,3354           54777                           TS       DSPCOUNT                              
019998,002527: 41,3355           31047                           CA       DSPTEM1    +2                         #  SUPERBANK BITS WERE PRELOADED INTO
019999,002528: 41,3356           54001                           TS       L                                     #  3RD COMPONENT OF NOUN 26.
020000,002529: 41,3357           31017                           CA       NOUNCADR                              #  ORIGINAL FCADR LOADED STILL IN NOUNCADR.
020001,002530: 41,3360           04651                           TC       SUPDACAL                              #  CALL WITH FCADR IN A, SUPERBITS IN L.
020002,002531: 41,3361           03363                           TC       DSPOCTWD                              
020003,002532: 41,3362           05155        ENDSPF             TC       ENDOFJOB

Page 463 

020433,002962:                                                                                                  #  KEY RELEASE ROUTINE
020434,002963: 
020435,002964:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE ALWAYS TURNS OFF THE UPACT LIGHT AND ALWAYS CLEARS DSPLOCK.
020436,002965: 
020437,002966:                                                                                                  #  THE HIGHEST PRIORITY FUNCTION OF THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON IS THE
020438,002967:                                                                                                  #  UNSUSPENDING OF A SUSPENDED MONITOR WHICH WAS EXTERNALLY INITIATED.
020439,002968:                                                                                                  #  THIS FUNCTION IS ACCOMPLISHED BY CLEARING DSPLOCK AND TURNING OFF
020440,002969:                                                                                                  #  THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT IF BOTH DSPLIST AND CADRSTOR ARE EMPTY.
020441,002970: 
020442,002971:                                                                                                  #  IF NO SUCH MONITOR EXISTS, THEN RELDSP IS EXECUTED TO CLEAR DSPLOCK
020443,002972:                                                                                                  #  AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (FREEING THE DISPLAY SYSTEM FOR INTERNAL
020444,002973:                                                                                                  #  USE), TURN OFF THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT, AND WAKE UP ANY JOB IN DSPLIST.
020445,002974: 
020446,002975:                                                                                                  #  IN ADDITION IF THERE IS A JOB IN ENDIDLE, THEN CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED
020447,002976:                                                                                                  #  TO PINBRNCH (IN DISPLAY INTERFACE ROUTINE) TO RE-EXECUTE THE SERIES OF
020448,002977:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CALLS ETC. THAT PRECEDED THE ENDIDLE CALL STILL AWAITING RESPONSE.
020449,002978:                                                                                                  #  THIS FEATURE IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN THE OPERATOR HAS BEEN REQUESTED TO
020450,002979:                                                                                                  #  RESPOND TO SOME INTERNAL ACTION THAT USED ENDIDLE, BUT HE HAS WRITTEN
020451,002980:                                                                                                  #  OVER THE INFORMATION ON THE DISPLAY PANEL BY SOME DISPLAYS OF HIS OWN
020452,002981:                                                                                                  #  INITIATION WHICH DO NOT SERVE AS RESPONSES. HITTING KEY RLSE WILL
020453,002982:                                                                                                  #  RE-ESTABLISH THE DISPLAYS TO THE STATE THEY WERE IN BEFORE HE OBSCURED
020454,002983:                                                                                                  #  THEM, SO THAT HE CAN SEE THE WAITING REQUEST.  THIS WORKS ONLY FOR
020455,002984:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL PROGRAMS THAT USED ENDIDLE THROUGH MARGARETS DISPLAY
020456,002985:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES.
020457,002986: 
020458,002987: 40,3457           44751        VBRELDSP           CS       BIT3                                  
020459,002988: 40,3460           00006                           EXTEND                                         
020460,002989: 40,3461           03011                           WAND     DSALMOUT                              #  TURN OFF UPACT LITE
020461,002990: 40,3462           10115                           CCS      21/22REG                              #  OLD DSPLOCK
020462,002991: 40,3463           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
020463,002992: 40,3464           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT (EMB)
020464,002993: 40,3465           10000                           CCS      A                                     
020465,002994: 40,3466           03475                           TC       UNSUSPEN                              #  OLD DSPLOCK AND EMB BOTH 1, UNSUSPEND.
020466,002995: 40,3467           04457        TSTLTS4            TC       RELDSP                                #  NOT UNSUSPENDING EXTERNAL MONITOR,
020467,002996: 40,3470           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   RELEASE DISPLAY SYSTEM AND
020468,002997: 40,3471           03473                           TC       +2                                    #   DO RE-ESTABLISH IF CADRSTOR IS FULL.
020469,002998: 40,3472           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020470,002999: 40,3473           04635                           TC       POSTJUMP                              
020471,003000: 40,3474           20723                           CADR     PINBRNCH                              
020472,003001: 40,3475           34755        UNSUSPEN           CAF      ZERO                                  #  EXTERNAL MONITOR IS SUSPENDED,
020473,003002: 40,3476           55012                           TS       DSPLOCK                               #   JUST UNSUSPEND IT BY CLEARING DSPLOCK.
020474,003003: 40,3477           11042                           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #   TURN KEY RELEASE LIGHT OFF IF BOTH
020475,003004: 40,3500           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              #   CADRSTOR AND DSPLIST ARE EMPTY.
020476,003005: 40,3501           04502                           TC       RELDSP1                               
020477,003006: 40,3502           05155                           TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020478,003007: 
020479,003008: 40,3503                        ENDRELDS           EQUALS                                         
020480,003009:

Page 464 

020482,003011:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IS USED FOR SUB ROUTINE CALLS FROM WITHIN COMPUTER. IT CAN BE
020483,003012:                                                                                                  #  USED TO CALL THE COMBINATION OF ANY DISPLAY, LOAD, OR MONITOR VERB
020484,003013:                                                                                                  #  TOGETHER WITH ANY NOUN AVAILABLE TO THE KEYBOARD.
020485,003014:                                                                                                  #  PLACE 0VVVVVVVNNNNNNN INTO A.
020486,003015:                                                                                                  #  V-S ARE THE 7 BIT VERB CODE.  N-S ARE THE 7 BIT NOUN CODE.
020487,003016: 
020488,003017:                                                                                                  #  IF NVSUB IS CALLED WITH THE FOLLOWING NEGATIVE NUMBERS (RATHER THAN THE
020489,003018:                                                                                                  #  VERB-NOUN CODE) IN A, THEN THE DISPLAY IS BLANKED AS FOLLOWS-
020490,003019:                                                                                                  #   -4 FULL BLANK, -3 LEAVE MODE, -2 LEAVE MODE AND VERB, -1 BLANK R-S ONLY
020491,003020: 
020492,003021:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB CAN BE USED WITH MACH CADR TO BE SPEC BY PLACING THE CADR INTO
020493,003022:                                                                                                  #  MPAC+2 BEFORE THE STANDARD NVSUB CALL.
020494,003023: 
020495,003024:                                                                                                  #   NVSUB RETURNS TO 2+ CALLING LOC AFTER PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020496,003025:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS AVAILABLE. THE NEW NOUN AND VERB CODES ARE DISPLAYED.
020497,003026:                                                                                                  #  IF V:S =0, THE NEW NOUN CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO FURTHER
020498,003027:                                                                                                  #  ACTION). IF N-S =0, THE NEW VERB CODE IS DISPLAYED ONLY(RETURN WITH NO
020499,003028:                                                                                                  #  FURTHER ACTION).
020500,003029: 
020501,003030:                                                                                                  #  IT RETURNS TO 1+ CALLING LOC WITHOUT PERFORMING TASK, IF DISPLAY
020502,003031:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS BLOCKED (NOTHING IS DISPLAYED IN THIS CASE).
020503,003032:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES TC ABORT (WITH OCT 01501) IF IT ENCOUNTERS A DISPLAY PROGRAM
020504,003033:                                                                                                  #  ALARM CONDITION BEFORE RETURN TO CALLER.
020505,003034: 
020506,003035:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS BLOCKED BY THE DEPRESSION OF ANY
020507,003036:                                                                                                  #  KEY, EXCEPT ERROR LIGHT RESET
020508,003037:                                                                                                  #  IT IS RELEASED BY THE KEY RELEASE BUTTON, ALL EXTENDED VERBS,
020509,003038:                                                                                                  #  PROCEED WITHOUT DATA, TERMINATE, RESEQUENCE, INITIALIZE EXECUTIVE,
020510,003039:                                                                                                  #  RECALL PART OF RECALTST IF ENDIDLE WAS USED,
020511,003040:                                                                                                  #  VB = REQUEST EXECUTIVE, VB = REQUEST WAITLIST,
020512,003041:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR SET UP.
020513,003042: 
020514,003043:                                                                                                  #  THE DISPLAY SYSTEM IS ALSO BLOCKED BY THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT, WHICH
020515,003044:                                                                                                  #  INDICATES AN EXTERNALLY INITIATED MONITOR IS RUNNING (SEE MONITOR)
020516,003045: 
020517,003046:                                                                                                  #  A NVSUB CALL THAT PASSES DSPLOCK AND THE EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT ENDS OLD
020518,003047:                                                                                                  #  MONITOR.
020519,003048: 
020520,003049:                                                                                                  #  DSPLOCK IS THE INTERLOCK FOR USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY SYSTEM WHICH
020521,003050:                                                                                                  #  LOCKS OUT INTERNAL USE WHENEVER THERE IS EXTERNAL KEYBOARD ACTION.
020522,003051: 
020523,003052:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB SHOULD BE USED TWICE IN SUCCESSION FOR :PLEASE PERFORM: SITUATIONS
020524,003053:                                                                                                  #  (SIMILARLY FOR PLEASE MARK). FIRST PLACE THE CODED NUMBER FOR WHAT
020525,003054:                                                                                                  #  ACTION IS DESIRED OF OPERATOR INTO THE REGISTERS REFERRED TO BY THE
020526,003055:                                                                                                  #  :CHECKLIST: NOUN. GO TO NVSUB WITH A DISPLAY VERB AND THE :CHECKLIST:
020527,003056:                                                                                                  #  NOUN. GO TO NVSUB AGAIN WITH THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB AND ZEROS IN THE
020528,003057:                                                                                                  #  LOW 7 BITS. THIS :PASTES UP: THE :PLEASE PERFORM: VERB INTO THE VERB
020529,003058:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS.
020530,003059: 
020531,003060:                                                                                                  #  NVMONOPT IS AN ENTRY SIMILAR TO NVSUB, BUT REQUIRING AN ADDITIONAL

Page 465 

020533,003062:                                                                                                  #  PARAMETER IN L. IT SHOULD BE USED ONLY WITH A MONITOR VERB-NOUN CODE IN
020534,003063:                                                                                                  #  A. AFTER EACH MONITOR DISPLAY A *PLEASE* VERB WILL BE PASTED IN THE VERB
020535,003064:                                                                                                  #  LIGHTS OR DATA WILL BE BLANKED (OR BOTH) ACCORDING TO THE OPTIONS
020536,003065:                                                                                                  #  SPECIFIED IN L. IF BITS 8-14 OF L ARE OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL 
020537,003066:                                                                                                  #  BE INTERPRETED AS A VERB CODE AND PASTED IN THE VERB LIGHTS. (THIS VERB
020538,003067:                                                                                                  #  CODE SHOULD DESIGNATE ONE OF THE *PLEASE* VERBS.) IF BITS 1-3 OF L ARE
020539,003068:                                                                                                  #  OTHER THAN ZERO, THEN THEY WILL BE USED TO BLANK DATA BY BEING FED TO
020540,003069:                                                                                                  #  BLANKSUB. IF NVMONOPT IS USED WITH A VERB OTHER THAN A MONITOR VERB,
020541,003070:                                                                                                  #  THE PARAMETER IN L HAS NO EFFECT.
020542,003071: 
020543,003072:                                                                                                  #  NVSUB IN FIXED-FIXED PLACES 2+CALLING LOC INTO NVQTEM, TC NVSUBEND INTO
020544,003073:                                                                                                  #  ENTRET. (THIS WILL RESTORE OLD CALLING BANK BITS)
020545,003074: 
020546,003075:    4154                                           SETLOC   ENDALM     +1                         
020547,003076: 
020548,003077:    4154                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN

020660,003189:    4205           55021                           TS       MONSAVE1                              #  TURN OFF BIT 14, THE EXTERNAL
020661,003190:                                                                                                  #   MONITOR BIT.
020662,003191:    4206           00002                           TC       Q                                     
020663,003192: 
020664,003193: 
020665,003194:                                                                                                  #  LOADSTAT  +0 INACTIVE(WAITING FOR DATA). SET BY NVSUB
020666,003195:                                                                                                  #            +1  PROCEED NO DATA. SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020667,003196:                                                                                                  #           -1 TERMINATE   SET BY SPECIAL VERB
020668,003197:                                                                                                  #           -0    DATA IN      SET BY END OF LOAD ROUTINE
020669,003198:                                                                                                  #              OR RESEQUENCE   SET BY VERB 32
020670,003199: 
020671,003200: 
020672,003201:                                                                                                  #  L  TO ENDIDLE  (FIXED FIXED)
020673,003202:                                                                                                  #  ROUTINES THAT REQUEST LOADS THROUGH NVSUB SHOULD USE ENDIDLE WHILE
020674,003203:                                                                                                  #  WAITING FOR THE DATA TO BE LOADED. ENDIDLE PUTS CURRENT JOB TO SLEEP.
020675,003204:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
020676,003205:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
020677,003206:                                                                                                  #  RECALTST TESTS LOADSTAT AND WAKES JOB UP TO,
020678,003207:                                                                                                  #  L+1      FOR TERMINATE
020679,003208:                                                                                                  #  L+2      FOR PROCEED WITHOUT DATA
020680,003209:                                                                                                  #  L+3      FOR DATA IN, OR RESEQUENCE
020681,003210:                                                                                                  #  IT DOES NOTHING IF LOADSTAT INDICATES WAITING FOR DATA.
020682,003211: 
020683,003212: 
020684,003213:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO SLEEP

Page 468 

020686,003215:                                                                                                  #  IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO ENDIDLE WHEN
020687,003216:                                                                                                  #  1) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF ENDIDLE IS
020688,003217:                                                                                                  #  EXCEEDED. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
020689,003218:                                                                                                  #  2) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO
020690,003219:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY.
020691,003220: 
020692,003221:    4207           22002        ENDIDLE            LXCH     Q                                     #  RETURN ADDRESS INTO L.
020693,003222:    4210           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0
020694,003223:    4211           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0
020695,003224:    4212           30001                           CA       L                                     #  DONT SET DSPLOCK TO 1 SO CAN USE
020696,003225:    4213           75012                           MASK     LOW10                                 #  ENDIDLE WITH NVSUB INITIATED MONITOR.
020697,003226:    4214           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  SAME STRATEGY FOR CADR AS MAKECADR.
020698,003227:    4215           55042                           TS       CADRSTOR                              
020699,003228:    4216           05133                           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
020700,003229: 
020701,003230: 
020702,003231:    4217           05155        ENDINST            TC       ENDOFJOB                              
020703,003232: 
020704,003233: 
020705,003234:    4220           11042        ISCADR+0           CCS      CADRSTOR                              #  ABORTS (CODE 01206) IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
020706,003235:    4221           04227                           TC       DSPABORT                              #  RETURNS IF CADRSTOR = +0.

020814,003343: 
020815,003344:                                                                                                  #  DSPMM DOES NOT DISPLAY MODREG DIRECTLY. IT PUTS IN EXEC REQUEST WITH
020816,003345:                                                                                                  #  PRIO 30000 FOR DSPMMJB AND RETURNS TO CALLER.

020819,003348:
