021047,003576:                                                                                                  #  INTERNAL USE OF KEYBOARD AND DISPLAY PROGRAM
021048,003577: 
021049,003578:                                                                                                  #  USER MUST SCHEDULE CALLS TO NVSUB SO THAT THERE IS NO CONFLICT OF USE OR
021050,003579:                                                                                                  #  CONFUSION TO OPERATOR. THE OLD GRABLOCK (INTERNAL/INTERNAL INTERLOCK)
021051,003580:                                                                                                  #  HAS BEEN REMOVED AND THE INTERNAL USER NO LONGER HAS THE PROTECTION THIS
021052,003581:                                                                                                  #  OFFERED.
021053,003582: 
021054,003583:                                                                                                  #  THERE ARE TWO WAYS A JOB CAN BE PUT TO SLEEP BY THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021055,003584:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM.    1) BY ENDIDLE
021056,003585:                                                                                                  #              2) BY NVSUBUSY
021057,003586:                                                                                                  #  THE BASIC CONVENTION IS THAT ONLY ONE JOB WILL BE PERMITTED ASLEEP VIA
021058,003587:                                                                                                  #  THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM AT A TIME. IF A JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021059,003588:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP BY MEANS OF (1) OR (2) AND THERE IS ALREADY A JOB ASLEEP THAT WAS
021060,003589:                                                                                                  #  PUT TO SLEEP BY (1) OR (2), THEN AN ABORT IS CAUSED.
021061,003590: 
021062,003591: 
021063,003592:                                                                                                  #  THE CALLING SEQUENCE FOR NVSUB IS
021064,003593:                                                                                                  #           CAF    V/N
021065,003594:                                                                                                  #  L        TC     NVSUB
021066,003595:                                                                                                  #  L+1      RETURN HERE IF OPERATOR HAS INTERVENED
021067,003596:                                                                                                  #  L+2      RETURN HERE AFTER EXECUTION
021068,003597: 
021069,003598: 
021070,003599:                                                                                                  #        A ROUTINE CALLED  NVSUBUSY IS PROVIDED (USE IS OPTIONAL)  TO PUT
021071,003600:                                                                                                  #  YOUR JOB TO SLEEP UNTIL THE OPERATOR RELEASES THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY
021072,003601:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM. NVSUBUSY ALSO TURNS ON THE KEY RELEASE LIGHT.
021073,003602:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY CANNOT BE CALLED FROM ERASABLE OR F/F MEMORY,
021074,003603:                                                                                                  #  SINCE JOBSLEEP AND JOBWAKE CAN HANDLE ONLY FIXED BANKS.
021075,003604: 
021076,003605: 
021077,003606:                                                                                                  #         THE CALLING SEQUENCE IS
021078,003607:                                                                                                  #           CAF    WAKEFCADR
021079,003608:                                                                                                  #           TC     NVSUBUSY
021080,003609: 
021081,003610: 
021082,003611:                                                                                                  #  .
021083,003612: 
021084,003613: 
021085,003614:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY IS INTENDED FOR USE WHEN AN INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS THE OPERATOR
021086,003615:                                                                                                  #  IS USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM (BY HIS OWN INITIATION). IT IS
021087,003616:                                                                                                  #  NOT INTENDED FOR USE WHEN ONE INTERNAL PROGRAM FINDS ANOTHER INTERNAL 
021088,003617:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM USING THE KEYBOARD + DISPLAY PROGRAM.
021089,003618: 
021090,003619: 
021091,003620:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBUSY ABORTS (WITH CODE 01206) IF A SECOND JOB ATTEMPTS TO GO TO
021092,003621:                                                                                                  #  SLEEP IN PINBALL. IN PARTICULAR, IF AN ATTEMPT IS MADE TO GO TO NVSUBUSY
021093,003622:                                                                                                  #  WHEN
021094,003623:                                                                                                  #  1) DSPLIST NOT= +0. THIS IS THE CASE WHERE THE CAPACITY OF THE DSPLIST
021095,003624:                                                                                                  #     IS EXCEEDED.
021096,003625:                                                                                                  #  2) CADRSTOR NOT= +0. THIS INDICATES THAT A JOB IS ALREADY USING

Page 477 

021098,003627:                                                                                                  #  ENDIDLE. (+-NZ INDICATE A JOB IS ALREADY ASLEEP DUE TO ENDIDLE.)
021099,003628: 
021100,003629:    4437           44444        PRENVBSY           CS       2K+3                                  #  SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED
021101,003630:    4440           60002                           AD       Q                                     #  BANKS ONLY DESIRING THE FCADR OF(LOC
021102,003631:    4441           60004                           AD       FBANK                                 #  FROM WHICH THE TC PRENVBSY WAS DONE) -2
021103,003632:    4442           04635        NVSUBUSY           TC       POSTJUMP                              #  TO BE ENTERED.
021104,003633:    4443           10604                           CADR     NVSUBSY1                              
021105,003634:    4444           02003        2K+3               OCT      2003                                  
021106,003635: 
021107,003636:                                                                                                  #  NVSUBSY1 MUST BE IN BANK 27 OR LOWER, SO IT WILL PUT CALLER TO SLEEP
021108,003637:                                                                                                  #  WITH HIS PROPER SUPERBITS.
021109,003638: 
021110,003639: 04,2604                                           SETLOC   ENDSPMM    +1                         
021111,003640: 04,2604                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021112,003641: 04,2604           54001        NVSUBSY1           TS       L                                     
021113,003642: 04,2605           04220                           TC       ISCADR+0                              #  ABORT IF CADRSTOR NOT= +0.
021114,003643: 04,2606           04224                           TC       ISLIST+0                              #  ABORT IF DSPLIST NOT= +0.
021115,003644: 04,2607           04374                           TC       RELDSPON                              
021116,003645: 04,2610           30001                           CA       L                                     
021117,003646: 04,2611           55043                           TS       DSPLIST                               
021118,003647: 04,2612           05133        ENDNVBSY           TC       JOBSLEEP                              
021119,003648: 
021120,003649: 
021121,003650:                                                                                                  #  NVSBWAIT IS A SPECIAL ENTRANCE FOR ROUTINES IN FIXED BANKS ONLY. IF
021122,003651:                                                                                                  #  SYSTEM IS NOT BUSY, IT EXECUTES V/N AND RETURNS TO L+1 (L= LOC FROM
021123,003652:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE TC NVSBWAIT WAS DONE). IF SYSTEM IS BUSY, IT PUTS CALLING JOB
021124,003653:                                                                                                  #  TO SLEEP WITH L-1 GOING INTO LIST FOR EVENTUAL WAKING UP WHEN SYSTEM
021125,003654:                                                                                                  #  IS NOT BUSY.
021126,003655: 
021127,003656:    4445                                           SETLOC   NVSUBUSY   +3                         
021128,003657:    4445                                           COUNT*   $$/PIN                                
021129,003658:    4445           22007        NVSBWAIT           LXCH     7                                     #  ZERO NVMONOPT OPTIONS
021130,003659:    4446           54123                           TS       NVTEMP                                
021131,003660:    4447           34736                           CAF      BIT14                                 
021132,003661:    4450           71021                           MASK     MONSAVE1                              #  EXTERNAL MONITOR BIT
021133,003662:    4451           61012                           AD       DSPLOCK                               
021134,003663:    4452           10000                           CCS      A                                     
021135,003664:    4453           14455                           TCF      NVSBWT1                               #  BUSY
021136,003665:    4454           14164                           TCF      NVSBCOM                               #  FREE. NVSUB WILL SAVE L+1 FOR RETURN
021137,003666:                                                                                                  #  AFTER EXECUTION.
021138,003667:    4455           24002        NVSBWT1            INCR     Q                                     #  L+2. PRENVBSY WILL PUT L-1 INTO LIST AND
021139,003668:    4456           14437                           TCF      PRENVBSY                              #  GO TO SLEEP.
021140,003669: 
021141,003670: 
021142,003671:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP IS USED BY VBPROC, VBTERM, VBRQEXEC, VBRQWAIT, VBRELDSP, EXTENDED
021143,003672:                                                                                                  #  VERB DISPATCHER, VBRESEQ, RECALTST.
021144,003673:                                                                                                  #  RELDSP1 IS USED BY MONITOR SET UP, VBRELDSP.
021145,003674:    4457           56002        RELDSP             XCH      Q                                     #  SET DSPLOCK TO +0, TURN RELDSP LIGHT
021146,003675:    4460           54144                           TS       RELRET                                #  OFF, SEARCH DSPLIST
021147,003676:    4461           44736                           CS       BIT14

021293,003822:                                                                                                  #  ERROR LIGHT RESET (RSET) TURNS OFF,
021294,003823:                                                                                                  #  UPLINK ACTIVITY, AUTO, HOLD, FREE, OPERATOR ERROR,
021295,003824:                                                                                                  #  PROG ALM, TRACKER FAIL.
021296,003825:                                                                                                  #  LEAVES GIMBAL LOCK AND NO ATT ALONE.
021297,003826:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO ZEROES THE :TEST ALARM: OUT BIT, WHICH TURNS OFF STBY,RESTART.
021298,003827:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO SETS :CAUTION RESET: TO 1.
021299,003828:                                                                                                  #  IT ALSO FORCES BIT 12 OF ALL DSPTAB ENTRIES TO 1.
